 Sri Lanka entered the quarter-finals after beating Zimbabwe by 139 runs in the World Cup Group a league match on Thursday, thanks to a four-wicket haul of opener Tillakaratne Dilshan and a record first wicket partnership with Upul Tharanga
 dilashaan ne nauvaan ek divasiy shatak jadte hue 144 ran banaaye jabaki tharanga ne karier kii sarvshereshth 133 ran kii pari kheli
 Thanks to this, Sri Lanka scored 327 runs for six wickets
 jawaab main zimbabwe kii team 39 over main 188 ran par out ho gai
 After the bat, Dilshan flashed the ball and took four wickets for just four runs in three overs
 anbhavi aaf spinner muthya muralidharan ne nau over main 34 ran dekar teen wicket chatkaye
 Earlier, Zimbabwe captain Elton Chigumbura had to bear the brunt of the fielding decision by winning the toss
 dilashaan or tharanga ne 282 ran kii saajhedaari kii or ek divasiy cricket main 286 ran kii praarambhik wicket kii saajhedaari kaa ricard todane se chaar ran se peeche rah gaye
 Tharanga formed this partnership with Sanath Jayasuriya against England in Leeds in 2006
 ek divasiy cricket ke itihaas main yah chauthi sabase badi saajhedaari he
 Christopher Mpofu broke the partnership by grabbing Tharanga in the hands of Chigumbura in cover in the 45th over
 tharanga ne 141 gend kii pari main 17 chauke lagaaye
 In the next over, Dilshan off-spinner Prosper Utseya lost his wicket
 is 34 varshiya ballebaaj ne 131 gend kii pari main ek chakka or 16 chauke lagaaye
 Mpofu took four wickets for 64 runs
 srilanka ke chaar wicket 45 ran ke bheetar gir gaye
 In the second over, Dilshan opened his hands to fast bowler Tinashe Peniangara with three fours and a six
 tharanga ne bhi unka puraa saath dete hue mapophu ke ek over main teen chauke lagaaye
 Sri Lanka had scored 77 runs in 10 overs
 dilashaan ne chigumbura kii gend par cover main ek ran lekar apana shatak puraa kiya
 He faced 95 balls for this
 stadium main maujuud 3 xxrep 4 0 darshakon ne khadey hokar unka abhivadan kiya
 Tharanga set a new World Cup record of partnership for the first wicket by scoring another four off Peniangara
 unhone pakistan ke said anwar or vajahatulla vasti kaa 1999 main newjiland ke khilaaf manchester main banaaya 194 ran kaa ricard todaa
 Tharanga completed his tenth ODI century with the 12th four of his innings off Raymond Price, which is also his first century in the World Cup
 isse pehle unka sarvshereshth score 120 ran tha jo unhone england ke khilaaf 2006 main lords par banaaya tha
 Zimbabwe had a very good start and openers Brendan Taylor and Regis Chakabwa added 116 runs for the first wicket

 The batsman scored 61 runs in 61 balls with the help of three fours

 ) It is not unheard of that the auditors do not resign before or during the audit, but such an incident has hardly been heard for a long time
 haalanki, 2018 par gaur karen to yah saamaanya lagane lag saktaa he
 After all, auditors of about 200 listed Indian companies left their jobs in the midst of the audit
 audit se pehle yaa uske dauraan kisi auditor ke istipha dene ke yun to kai kaaran ho sakate hai; lekin audit maanak or aachaar samhita kaa maamla khadaa ho jaae to kisi auditor ko jarur istipha dena chahie
 But before taking this sentence further, it is important to keep in mind that the recent resignations of Anil Ambani-owned Reliance Capital and Reliance Home Finance Ltd auditor pwc are not an unusual incident
 ye to donon companiyon ke haai profile hone ke naate surkhiyon main aa gaye
 The resignation of the auditor in the middle of the audit creates a ruckus
 yah sanket detaa he ki company kii vyavastha main kuch baari gadabadi he
 This can lead to worry lines on the foreheads of its investors, lenders, creditors and other parties
 auditor ke istife se company or uske nideshak mandal kii pratishtha ko bhi dhakka pahunchataa he
 Therefore, auditors should try to complete the audit and present their report
 unke paas yah vikalp he ki ve koi shart (apni raay dene main asamarthta kaa hawala dekar) jod den yaa phir safagoi se report taiyaar kar den
 Resignation should be the last option - resigning without adequate reason is unethical and a violation of their professional obligations to shareholders and the public
 kuch saal pehle tak, istipha dekar kisi audit ko chhodie ke liye kaarnon kaa khulaasa karne kii aavashyaktaa nahin thi
 But the Companies Act 2013 changed that
 niamakon ke paas report daakhil karte vakt aisi kisi ghatana ke liye auditor or company, donon ko paryaapt vajah bataani hoti he
 Each party has the right to know why the auditors quit? pwc's resignation is of particular importance as it pertains to suspected fraud as per Section 143 (12) of the Companies Act 2013
 kanoon ke anusaar, kisi auditor ko audit ke dauraan yah vishwaas karne kaa thos kaaran miltaa he ki company ke adhikariyon yaa karmchaariyon ne ek karod rupye yaa usase adhik kii dhokhadhadi kii he, to use turant company kii audit cameti ko us sandigdh dhokhadhadi kii soochna deni chahie
 It is necessary for the audit committee to respond to the auditor within forty-five days or to express his opinion on that questionable subject
 lekha pareekshak ko us sandigdh dhokhadhadi kii jaankaree centre sarkaar ko deni chahie or audit cameti kii tippaniyon ke saath apni raay se sarkaar ko avgat karana chahie
 If he does not get the response of the audit committee, then he should send his report to the audit committee to the government
 peedblusi kaa aarope he ki reliance capital ne tay samay ke bheetar audit samiti kii baithak nahin bulaai; sambandhit companiyaan santoshjanak rup se 'kuch tippaniyon / lenden' ko saaf nahin kar sakin jo donon companiyon ke vittiya vivaranon ke liye mahatvapurn yaa aavashyak ho sakati hai; prabandhan dwaara audit ke dauraan kanoonee karrwai kii dhamkee di gai thi jiske kaaran unki audit karne kii kshamta par asar pad rahaa tha
 As such, he had no choice but to resign
 peedblusi ke istife ke baad pathak ech
 D
 and associats hi ab ekmaatr auditor ke rup main kaam jari rakhegi
 Even if the company's sole auditor gives him a clean chit and does not report the fraud, the pwc can still stand, because the pwc had only suspected the fraud, not the fraud
 haalanki, istife ke kaaran peedblusi ko mukademebaaji kaa jokhim uthaanaa pad saktaa he
 The company, its investors, creditors, directors and other stakeholders can sue for defamation, which is both civil and criminal
 ve aarope laga sakate hai ki istipha dene ke dauraan diya gaya bayaan galat or bhraamak tha or peedblusi ne surkhiyon main chadhgaye yaa badla lene jaise kisi nihit swaarth ke liye us bayaan kaa istemaal kiya, yaa uski niyat main khot tha
 It is difficult to say that pwc resigned in haste due to the legal action and the proposal for punitive action against the four big audit firms
 bhartiya pratibhuti or vinimay board (sebi), rashtriya vittiya reportig praadhikaran (enegaare) or anya niamak, dastavejon kii jaanch ke baad moolyankan karenge ki kya istipha uchit tha
 But it is also unlikely that pwc would not have prepared for all this

 yah ausat bharat main prati ek hajaar logon par aspataalon, skulon, police thanon, railway steshnon aadi kisi bhi saarvajanik seva se bahut bada he

 dharm ek saamudayik seva ke taur par bharat ko duniya se bilkul alag khadaa karata he

 bharat ke saamaajik-aarthik dhaanche main dharmik centre, ek vaastavik sampatti (tengibil asset) hai, jo saamaajik parivesh main bane rahane ke liye sansaadhan jutate hai, logon ko rojgaar dete hai or apni gatividhiyaan badhaakar majholi se badi arthvyavastha ban jate hai
 This community service of India on the basis of socio-economic property is a victim of three kinds of inconsistencies
 inamen pehali he kshamtaaon kii kami-bharat kii aabaadi ke sabase bade hisse ko dainik, saptahik masik or vaarshik aadhaar par seva dene vaale is tantra ke paas maang ke mutabik kshamtaayen nahin hai

 'rajarshi' do bacchon kii kahani se shuru hoti he
 The king also plays with these two children playing on the banks of the Rose River near a temple

 The king then prohibits the sacrifice in the kingdom, the monarchy stands against him, the king's own people plot against him and eventually the king has to fight a long and non-violent battle
 yah kaayade se gandhi se pehle gandhi kaa prayog tha jo gurudev apane upanyaas main kar rahe the
